# ## Format: This is a TAB-separated CSV. Character endoding is in Unicode (UTF-8)
# ## SentiStrength is using the first 2 fields only, all other fields are ignored.
# ### (i.e. nouns have to be written with uppercase initials).
# ### At the moment SentiStrength requires its lexica					
# ### CASE
# ### For proper fullform-generation this source *must* thus be kept case-sensitive 
# ### In order to generate inflected full-forms from the lemmata in this file use the following script:
# ### The morphological processing (FST) is case-sensitive though.  
# ### UMLAUT
# ### Umlauts should be written using Unicode-UTF8. The script for fullform-generation
# ### When editing the lexicon you should always edit THIS file. 
# ### lemmaLex2fullforms.pl -l de -c -u _EmotionLookupTable_v5_SOURCE.csv > EmotionLookupTable_v5_fullforms.txt
# ### to be lowercased! 					
# ### will produce also ASCII-only transcriptions as well (e.g. swill produce both 'süß' AND 'suess')    # # #
